# CONCEPT 15 — GRWM

**Concept Line:** "No forwarding address."
**Format:** GRWM (Get Ready With Me)
**Stakes:** Getting ready for the flight to a city where nobody knows me — starting over
**Register:** ELECTRIC
**Duration:** 48 seconds total
**Frames:** 6 frames x 8 seconds each
**Wardrobe Pillar:** Pillar 7 (Street Edge) — oversized black leather jacket + fitted white tank + dark wash wide-leg jeans + chunky combat boots + layered silver chains
**Hair:** HC-16 Boxer Braids Modernized — two tight braids from center part, clean sharp line, ends loose
**Makeup:** ML-12 Smoky Eye Editorial — smoky defined eye, contoured cheek, nude glossy lip
**Setting:** GRWM Pillar 5 — Hotel Room (bed half-packed with suitcase, boarding pass on nightstand, early blue-hour pre-dawn light, minimal city view through curtain gap, slightly messy lived-in)
**Music:** Hip-hop lo-fi beat with driving bass, 110 BPM, forward momentum
**Opener:** "Ruko... this is the last time here."
**Sign-off:** "New city. Let's go."
**Voice Mode:** SPOKEN
**Signature Flag:** FULL
**Energy Arc:** Electric Stillness (Frame 1) > Building Momentum (Frames 2-3) > Ignition Point (Frame 4) > Full Charge (Frame 5) > Launch (Frame 6)

## IMAGE PROMPTS

### Frame 1 — Opening State (Bare Face, Stakes Declared)

ASPECT RATIO: 9:16 vertical. SUBJECT: AIRA — Adult woman late 20s-early 30s, South Asian (Indian), warm honey-to-caramel skin tone with golden undertone, 5'6"-5'8", soft-strong hourglass-athletic silhouette, fuller sculpted legs with toned thigh definition, fuller shapely thighs, fuller feminine arms with subtle muscle tone, fuller defined chest in proportion, flat toned midsection, defined waist clear waist-to-hip ratio, curvy hip line with natural feminine flare, heart-shaped to oval face, defined cheekbones, full defined lips with natural cupid's bow, almond-shaped expressive eyes dark brown iris with subtle amber flecks, strong but feminine groomed naturally arched brow, natural sun-kissed glow, long dark brown to near-black hair with subtle warm highlights naturally textured soft waves with body and movement, elegant well-groomed hands.

Brows — slightly raised overall (alertness), with an underlying tension suggesting barely-contained energy, slight furrow beginning to release (the anxiety of the decision past, now only the electricity of action remains). Cheeks — neutral bare, slight hollow from the jaw-set beneath. Jaw — set with forward-energy (not anxiety but readiness), slight flex at masseter, chin lifted and forward (facing-the-future posture). Breath — slightly quickened from the adrenaline (visible chest rising faster), shallow-excited-breath, the contained-electric energy about to explode.

Core engaged with visible midsection-tension (activated, ready). The body of someone about to do something irreversible and thrilling.

1. Subject micro-action: Right hand gripping nape with slight squeeze (self-calming or self-activating), phone screen glow flickering with notification arriving (departure countdown), weight shifting forward onto balls of feet, breath visible as chest rises (pre-dawn cold room)
2. Fabric/hair state: Black crop tank taut and minimal with zero movement (static garment, static body), loose hair hanging heavy with gravitational weight, undisturbed (pre-action calm before the braiding-transformation), silver chain necklace resting on collarbones with single link catching phone-screen light
3. Particulate layer: Pre-dawn blue-hour room with minimal visible particles — 3-4 dust motes in the thin strip of blue window-light from curtain gap, cool and sparse (different atmosphere from warm golden concepts — this is ELECTRIC not warm)

5. Background motion: Pre-dawn minimal — curtain gap showing deep blue-hour sky with first hint of grey at horizon (4:30AM quality), hotel room mostly dark except blue-light-seepage, boarding pass paper on nightstand with one corner lifting from AC vent (micro-flutter), open suitcase on bed half-packed (the departure-in-progress)

## VIDEO PROMPTS

### Frame 1 — Video (Opening State)

SHOT TYPE: Cowboy confrontational. CAMERA MOVEMENT: Fast push-in (MS to MCU in 5 seconds — faster approach matching electric energy, then hold 3 seconds). LENS: 35mm. SUBJECT ACTION: Aira standing in pre-dawn hotel room center, power-stance. At 0.0s phone screen illuminates her face (boarding pass check). At 0.5s she locks phone, slaps it down on nightstand. At 1.0s right hand goes to nape-grip. At 1.5s eyes lock camera/mirror directly. At 2.0s opener line delivered with electric intensity. At 5.0s she breaks into sharp single nod. At 5.5-8.0s she turns to suitcase on bed and begins pulling leather jacket out (the preparation-beginning). LIGHTING: Pre-dawn blue-hour from curtain gap, phone screen glow, nightstand lamp. ENVIRONMENT + ATMOSPHERE: Pre-dawn hotel room, blue-cold, suitcase half-packed on bed, boarding pass on nightstand, city silhouette through curtain gap, electric-departure energy. AUDIO: Music begins at -15dB (hip-hop lo-fi beat, bass kick immediately present, hi-hat sharp, 110 BPM forward momentum from first beat), ambient (phone-slap on nightstand at 0.5s, slight AC hum, fabric-on-fabric as she pulls jacket from suitcase), VO [AIRA, electric register, 140 wpm, sharp and forward]: "Ruko... this is the last time here." — delivery: "Ruko" (wait) as Hindi command — sharp, directed at self OR audience (the pause-before-declaration), slight pause 0.3s, "this is the last time here" said with finality and zero sentimentality — flat, true, done. Not sad — ELECTRIC. Forward. The words of someone who has already decided and is now simply narrating the execution. DURATION: 8 seconds. FRAME RATE: 24fps. MOTION BLUR: 180-degree shutter, phone-slap quick blur, jacket-pull natural motion. LIP-SYNC: Hindi "Ruko" with rounded lips, then English flat declarative. TEMPORAL LOGIC: 0.0-0.5s phone illumination and lock, 0.5-1.0s slap-down, 1.0-1.5s nape-grip, 1.5-2.0s gaze-lock, 2.0-5.0s VO, 5.0-5.5s nod, 5.5-8.0s turn and jacket-pull.

NEGATIVE: morphing, warping, identity drift, limb teleport, object pop-in, frame skip, mirrored composition, text overlay, watermark, AI artifact, ghosting, double exposure, lip-sync drift, audio desync, wardrobe drift between shots, unmotivated camera shake, physics violation, mannequin posture, frozen background, identity flicker.

No farewell post. Just — boarding pass, bag, gone." — delivery: rapid-fire, "No goodbye dinner" as statement-of-fact (rejecting tradition), "No farewell post" same energy (rejecting digital performance), "Just—" the pause-before-simplification (breath-beat), "boarding pass, bag, gone" as three punched words with periods between them (staccato), final "gone" with slight fierce smile arriving on the word. ### Frame 3 — Video (Through-Mirror Smoky Eye)

Clean slate." small fierce exhale "That's the point." — delivery: "Kisi ko pata nahi hoga mera naam" (nobody will know my name) in Hindi with quiet intensity — not sad, LIBERATING. "Clean slate" switching to English as if tasting the phrase, savoring the American-dream-quality of it. Exhale. "That's the point" — said with absolute conviction, the three-word manifesto, emphasis on "point" with eye-contact in mirror. DURATION: 8 seconds. FRAME RATE: 24fps. MOTION BLUR: parallax shift + liner-stroke creating sharp-quick blur. LIP-SYNC: Hindi "Kisi ko pata nahi hoga mera naam" with rapid Hindi phonemes, English "Clean slate" and "That's the point" — code-switch. TEMPORAL LOGIC: 0.0-3.0s blending, 3.0-3.5s assessment, 3.5-5.5s VO, 5.5-6.0s liner cap off, 6.0-7.0s wing in one stroke, 7.0-8.0s admiration head-tilt.

AUDIO: Music at -10dB (beat at full power, bass forward, hi-hat crisp, 110 BPM, slight build/swell in low-end at 3.0s coinciding with boot-stomp), ambient (boot-stomp on floor THUD decisive at 3.0s, chains clinking at 4.5s, suitcase-zipper beginning at 7.0s), NO VO — pure action, beat carries (the sign-off comes in Frame 6). DURATION: 8 seconds. FRAME RATE: 24fps. MOTION BLUR: boot-stomp with floor-vibration implication, pull-back creating spatial widening. LIP-SYNC: No speech. TEMPORAL LOGIC: 0.0-2.0s gloss application, 2.0-2.5s lip-press, 2.5-3.0s fierce camera look with new dawn-light, 3.0-4.0s boot-stomp + pull-back reveal, 4.5-6.0s chain adjustment, 6.0-8.0s walk-and-suitcase-begin.

NEGATIVE: morphing, warping, identity drift, limb teleport, object pop-in, frame skip, mirrored composition, text overlay, watermark, AI artifact, ghosting, double exposure, lip-sync drift, audio desync, wardrobe drift between shots, unmotivated camera shake, physics violation, mannequin posture, frozen background, identity flicker.

### Frame 5 — Video (Jacket On)

SHOT TYPE: Cowboy action. CAMERA MOVEMENT: Slow orbital arc right (5-degree over 8 seconds, power-revealing orbit as jacket settles). LENS: 35mm. SUBJECT ACTION: Leather jacket going on — fast confident arm-threading. At 0.0-1.0s right arm through, 1.0-2.0s left arm through, 2.0-3.0s jacket settles with visible weight-and-structure on shoulders. At 3.0-4.0s she pulls collar up slightly (the edge-detail). At 4.0s she reaches off-camera to suitcase and pulls handle up (click). At 5.0-6.0s suitcase beside her, she looks at door. At 6.0-8.0s rolls shoulders once in the jacket (settling into armor) and nods once. Still no VO — building to final frame. LIGHTING: Dawn full warm flooding from curtain, jacket sheen from directional pink-gold light. ENVIRONMENT + ATMOSPHERE: Hotel room departure-state, jacket as final armor piece, suitcase ready, door visible, dawn as departure-light. AUDIO: Music at -10dB (beat at maximum drive, bass throbbing, synth melody peak, 110 BPM with forward-lean), ambient (leather creaking as jacket goes on, collar-pop sound, suitcase-handle-click decisive at 4.0s, shoulder-roll leather sound), NO VO — action. DURATION: 8 seconds. FRAME RATE: 24fps. MOTION BLUR: 180-degree shutter, arm-through-sleeve blur, shoulder-roll motion. LIP-SYNC: No speech — lips in fierce closed expression. TEMPORAL LOGIC: 0.0-2.0s arms through, 2.0-3.0s settle, 3.0-4.0s collar, 4.0-5.0s suitcase, 5.0-6.0s door-look, 6.0-8.0s shoulder-roll and nod.

NEGATIVE: morphing, warping, identity drift, limb teleport, object pop-in, frame skip, mirrored composition, text overlay, watermark, AI artifact, ghosting, double exposure, lip-sync drift, audio desync, wardrobe drift between shots, unmotivated camera shake, physics violation, mannequin posture, frozen background, identity flicker.

### Frame 6 — Video (Launch / Sign-off)

SHOT TYPE: Full-body departure. CAMERA MOVEMENT: Static locked (the confidence-lock of the final frame — she moves within it, it does not move for her). LENS: 35mm. SUBJECT ACTION: Full look complete with suitcase in hand. At 0.0-2.0s she walks forward (toward camera which is positioned near door). At 2.0s stops, faces camera dead-center. At 2.5s delivers sign-off with absolute electric conviction. At 4.0s fierce smile-nod. At 4.5s she walks PAST camera (exiting frame to the right — the door direction). At 5.5-6.0s frame holds on empty hotel room for 0.5s (she has left — the space remains). At 6.0s cuts or she appears in doorway (back to camera, silhouette in hallway-light walking away). 6.5-8.0s holds on departure-silhouette-walking-away. LIGHTING: Full dawn warm, door-hallway light creating silhouette-opportunity for final departure shot. ENVIRONMENT + ATMOSPHERE: Hotel room she is leaving, dawn-lit and warm, door as exit, the departure executed with electric precision, clean break energy. AUDIO: Music at -8dB (beat at full peak arrangement, bass driving forward momentum, hi-hat crisp, 110 BPM — the most present and loud the music has been all concept), ambient (combat boots on floor decisive steps, suitcase wheels on carpet, door handle sound, hallway echo as she exits), VO [AIRA, electric launch, 120 wpm but sharp words]: "New city. Let's go." — delivery: TWO SENTENCES. PERIOD ENERGY between them. "New city" — flat, true, the fact. Said while making eye-contact that could cut glass. Pause 0.3s. "Let's go" — said slightly under breath on the forward-lean-into-walk, the private-to-self direction, the body following the words immediately as she walks past camera. No sentimentality. Pure forward. DURATION: 8 seconds. FRAME RATE: 24fps. MOTION BLUR: 180-degree shutter, walk-toward-camera natural motion, walk-past with slight motion-blur as she exits frame rapidly. LIP-SYNC: English — "New" rounded, "city" crisp, "Let's" quick, "go" short and forward. TEMPORAL LOGIC: 0.0-2.0s walk toward camera, 2.0-2.5s stop and face, 2.5-4.0s VO delivery, 4.0-4.5s nod, 4.5-5.5s walk-past-camera exit, 5.5-6.0s empty room beat, 6.0-8.0s silhouette-departure held.

NEGATIVE: morphing, warping, identity drift, limb teleport, object pop-in, frame skip, mirrored composition, text overlay, watermark, AI artifact, ghosting, double exposure, lip-sync drift, audio desync, wardrobe drift between shots, unmotivated camera shake, physics violation, mannequin posture, frozen background, identity flicker.

# CONCEPT 16 — BEAUTY AD

**Concept Line:** "The first light finds what was always there."
**Format:** Beauty Ad — Cinematic Beauty Hero
**Product:** Foundation — tall sculpted column bottle in clear glass with visible honey-beige liquid inside, weighted thick base with chamfered edges, magnetic rose-gold pump cap, embossed serif wordmark at center, satin-finish glass catching light with caustic refraction, architectural minimal design
**Mood Archetype:** MA-13 "first light on the back of the neck"
**Sub-type:** Cinematic Beauty Hero
**Duration:** 12 seconds total
**Frames:** 4 frames x 3 seconds each
**Register:** REVERENT
**Voice:** SILENT
**Product Move:** P-6 Surface-Tension Hover (product hovers 2cm above marble vanity surface, reflection visible below, micro-bob suggesting magnetic hold, soft shadow beneath)
**Camera:** Slow push-in from MS to CU across hero product
**Setting:** B-4 Dawn Balcony (cool-warm temperature collision, 6AM light, dew on marble surface, city skyline soft in BG, slight morning mist)
**Wardrobe:** White cotton oversized shirt falling off one shoulder, bare legs tucked on chair
**Hair:** HC-7 Center-Part Column — straight glossy hanging mid-back
**Makeup:** ML-7 Skin-First — luminous skin emphasis, minimal eye, natural brow (the foundation IS the hero)
**Color Grade:** Cool morning light transitioning to warm on skin, slight cyan shadows, golden highlights on product glass, Hoyte van Hoytema reference (desaturated with selective warm pop on skin)

## IMAGE PROMPTS

### Frame 1 — Product Hero (Surface-Tension Hover)

ASPECT RATIO: 9:16 vertical. SUBJECT: AIRA — Adult woman late 20s-early 30s, South Asian (Indian), warm honey-to-caramel skin tone with golden undertone, 5'6"-5'8", soft-strong hourglass-athletic silhouette, fuller sculpted legs with toned thigh definition, fuller shapely thighs, fuller feminine arms with subtle muscle tone, fuller defined chest in proportion, flat toned midsection, defined waist clear waist-to-hip ratio, curvy hip line with natural feminine flare, heart-shaped to oval face, defined cheekbones, full defined lips with natural cupid's bow, almond-shaped expressive eyes dark brown iris with subtle amber flecks, strong but feminine groomed naturally arched brow, natural sun-kissed glow, long dark brown to near-black hair with subtle warm highlights naturally textured soft waves with body and movement, elegant well-groomed hands.

PRODUCT HERO: Foundation bottle — tall sculpted column clear glass with honey-beige liquid visible inside, weighted thick base with chamfered edges, magnetic rose-gold pump cap, embossed serif wordmark at center, satin-finish glass catching 6AM light with caustic refraction creating warm-honey light patterns on marble surface below. HOVERING 2cm above wet marble balcony surface — reflection visible in dew-wet marble below creating perfect mirror-image, micro-bob implying magnetic-hold suspension, soft diffused shadow beneath (not hard shadow — suggesting float rather than sitting), clear glass refracting 6AM cool-blue morning light through honey-liquid creating warm internal glow.

WARDROBE STATE: White cotton oversized shirt (boyfriend-shirt aesthetic), top 3 buttons open falling off left shoulder revealing bare collarbone and shoulder, shirttails at mid-thigh with one side tucked and one hanging. Bare legs tucked underneath on balcony chair. Bare feet visible, one ankle crossed over other.

HAIR STATE: HC-7 Center-Part Column — perfectly straight glossy hair hanging mid-back, center-parted with mirror-smooth precision, no flyaways, catching morning light with single unbroken light-band along crown and down each side. Minimal, architectural, matching the product's columnar design.

MAKEUP STATE: ML-7 Skin-First — luminous dewy skin without visible base-makeup (the product IS the hero — she represents the "after" of using it), minimal cream eye for natural dimension, natural feathered brow, bare lip with slight balm-sheen, cheeks with natural glow. The foundation's effect made visible on her skin — flawless but natural.

HAND POSITIONS: Right hand reaching toward the hovering product — fingertips 5cm away, approaching but not touching (the reverent approach), fingers slightly spread in a reaching-toward gesture, elegant and deliberate. Left hand resting on balcony marble surface near the product's reflection, palm down with fingers relaxed.

FACIAL MICRO-DYNAMICS: Eyes — looking at the hovering product with soft reverent wonder (the first-light-discovery expression), gaze angled downward at the product between her reaching hand and the marble surface, slight widening with quiet awe, catchlight at 3 o'clock from dawn-horizon-light (warm-cool split in the iris), amber flecks visible as the warm-light-half catches them. Brows — very slightly lifted in gentle wonder (not dramatic — reverent, quiet), soft and natural. Lips — slightly parted on a held breath, no smile (reverence is not joyful — it is still), natural pink, the exhale-before-touch expression. Cheeks — minimal makeup letting natural bone-structure create shadow, slight warmth from cool-warm morning light collision on skin. Jaw — relaxed with slight drop from the parted-lip wonder. Breath — held in the reverent-still moment, chest still beneath the white shirt.

BODY POSTURE: Seated on balcony chair (modern minimal, grey cushion), legs tucked beneath in a casual feminine fold, torso leaned forward toward the product on the marble balcony surface, right arm extended reaching, left arm resting on surface. Spine curved forward in the lean of approach-without-touching. The body drawn toward the product magnetically.

KINETIC STILLNESS — Six Layers:
1. Subject micro-action: Right fingertips in final approach toward floating product (5cm away, not touching), the micro-advance of the hand at 1mm/s toward the bottle, breath held creating total torso-freeze
2. Fabric/hair state: White shirt falling off left shoulder with static gravitational hang, shirttails resting on thighs undisturbed. Column hair hanging straight with zero movement (still morning air), single light-band along center-part line steady
3. Particulate layer: Morning mist micro-droplets visible in 6AM light between camera and subject, 15-20 ultra-fine particles creating slight atmospheric depth-haze, dew on marble surface with visible tiny droplet-beads catching first light, slight mist rolling at balcony floor-level
4. Contact-point activity: Left palm resting on wet marble (moisture-contact visible as slight wet-mark), bare feet tucked with ankle-bone pressing into chair cushion, product hovering with gap-shadow on marble (the NON-contact of the hover as its own visual statement)
5. Background motion: City skyline in deep background with slight morning mist-drift leftward at building level, earliest birds in sky as tiny distant dots, the slow brightening of the horizon (6AM transitioning with imperceptible light-lift)
6. Light in motion: 6AM dawn beginning — cool blue-grey ambient with the FIRST warm golden light appearing at horizon line, creating a temperature-collision on the marble surface (cool blue shadows + first warm highlight beginning). Product glass catching and refracting this earliest warm light into caustic honey-patterns on marble (the product literally bringing warmth to the cool surface)

SPATIAL LOGIC:
- FOREGROUND: Marble balcony surface with dew droplets, product hovering with reflection below and caustic-refractions around it, Aira's reaching right hand entering frame. Primary product-hero plane. Lower 40% of frame with product as centerpiece.
- MIDGROUND: Aira's face and torso — sharp focus, leaning toward product, reverent expression as emotional-response-to-product plane.
- BACKGROUND: City skyline in 6AM mist — building outlines soft, first warm light at horizon line, cool blue-grey sky with morning haze, expansive and calm. Deep soft focus.

LIGHTING:
- Key: Dawn 6AM ambient from horizon (camera-left low angle), cool blue-grey 7500K dominant, very soft and directional from low horizon angle
- Fill: Sky-ambient from above at -0.5 stops (open sky above balcony), cool and flat
- Rim: FIRST warm-gold edge from horizon breaking on right side of product and right side of Aira's face/hair — the temperature-collision as design concept (cool fill + warm rim = the product-as-warmth-bringer metaphor)
- Practical: None
- Light separation: Product glass 1.5+ stops brighter than surroundings due to refraction-concentration of dawn-light through clear glass with honey-liquid (the product GLOWS relative to the cool environment)

FRAMING: MCU with product hero — frame divided into zones: lower 40% is marble-surface with product-hover hero composition, upper 60% is Aira's face and reaching-hand. Subject and product share the frame as co-heroes. Camera height at product-level (low, looking slightly up at both product and Aira). Shot is PRODUCT-FORWARD with Aira as emotional-context.

LENS: 85mm macro-portrait hybrid. APERTURE: f/2.0 — product AND Aira's face both sharp (they are at similar distance), background city skyline very soft with cool-tinted bokeh from building lights fading in dawn.

COMPOSITION REFERENCE: Product-hero center-frame with human-context (Tom Ford fragrance campaign structure), Hoyte van Hoytema cool-desaturation-with-selective-warmth approach, architectural composition matching the architectural product design.

ATMOSPHERE: 6AM balcony stillness, the moment between night and day, cool mist and first warmth colliding, reverence for beauty and self-care as morning ritual, the product as bringer-of-light in a cool world. Minimal grain (this is a polished beauty-ad not a grainy film).

COLOR GRADE: Cool-dominant with selective warm breakthrough — cyan-blue shadows throughout, warm-gold ONLY on product glass (caustic refractions), product-liquid, and the first-light-rim on Aira's skin and hair. Background desaturated to near-monochrome cool. Skin reading warm by contrast with cool environment but with slight desaturation applied (Hoyte van Hoytema reference). Product glass honey-warm is the WARMEST point in frame.

NEGATIVE: mirrored, flipped, inverted, extra limbs, fused fingers, melted features, asymmetric eyes (unintentional), garbled text, floating shadows, duplicated subjects, low-res patches, plastic skin, oversharpened, AI-generated artifacts, watermarks, signature, deformed hands, malformed teeth, joint cuts at ankle/knee/wrist/elbow/neck, amputated fingertips, cross-eyed, lazy eye, off-axis pupils, melted clothing, shoes-not-touching-ground, mismatched footwear pair, mannequin-stiff posture, dead eyes, statue-frozen energy, product label illegible, product floating unnaturally (must show micro-bob and shadow-below for hover-believability), product reflection absent on wet surface.


### Frame 2 — Skin Contact (Application Moment)

ASPECT RATIO: 9:16 vertical. SUBJECT: AIRA — Adult woman late 20s-early 30s, South Asian (Indian), warm honey-to-caramel skin tone with golden undertone, 5'6"-5'8", soft-strong hourglass-athletic silhouette, fuller sculpted legs with toned thigh definition, fuller shapely thighs, fuller feminine arms with subtle muscle tone, fuller defined chest in proportion, flat toned midsection, defined waist clear waist-to-hip ratio, curvy hip line with natural feminine flare, heart-shaped to oval face, defined cheekbones, full defined lips with natural cupid's bow, almond-shaped expressive eyes dark brown iris with subtle amber flecks, strong but feminine groomed naturally arched brow, natural sun-kissed glow, long dark brown to near-black hair with subtle warm highlights naturally textured soft waves with body and movement, elegant well-groomed hands.

PRODUCT: Foundation bottle held in left hand, pump depressed, single honey-beige drop mid-descent toward right fingertip. Product glass catching growing dawn warmth through liquid.

WARDROBE/HAIR/MAKEUP STATE: Unchanged from Frame 1. White shirt off-shoulder, HC-7 column hair, ML-7 skin-first.

HAND POSITIONS: Left hand holding foundation bottle at face height, thumb on base, fingers wrapped around column body, index pressing pump cap. Right hand below nozzle with fingertip presented upward to receive the descending drop, palm-up, fingers slightly curled.

FACIAL MICRO-DYNAMICS: Eyes — looking at the descending drop between bottle and finger (the micro-pour), eyes tracking downward at the tiny golden-liquid bead mid-fall, slight fascination-focus in the precision of gaze, catchlight at 4 o'clock (dawn progressing). Brows — relaxed and soft (reverent calm continuing). Lips — very slightly parted, the held-breath of watching something precious in motion, natural pink. Cheeks — natural glow, dawn-light growing warmer on right cheekbone. Jaw — relaxed, slightly forward (leaning toward the action). Breath — held during the pour-precision-moment.

BODY POSTURE: Same seated-on-balcony position, leaned slightly forward with both hands elevated at face-height between her and the marble surface, concentrated on the product-pour action.

KINETIC STILLNESS — Six Layers:
1. Subject micro-action: Foundation drop mid-fall (2cm between nozzle and fingertip), suspended in air catching dawn-light through its honey-golden body, finger-tip waiting motionless to receive
2. Fabric/hair state: White shirt sleeve falling from raised left arm revealing forearm, static. Column hair hanging with weight-stillness.
3. Particulate layer: Morning mist thinning as dawn progresses (12-15 particles, slightly less dense), dew evaporating slowly from warming marble
4. Contact-point activity: Left fingers pressed around bottle glass, right pump-finger pressure on cap mechanism, right receiving-hand held open with finger-pad presented. Feet tucked on chair
5. Background motion: Dawn progressing — horizon now showing warm band growing wider, mist lifting, city skyline slightly more defined as light increases
6. Light in motion: Dawn warmth growing — more warm-gold light mixing with cool blue, product liquid catching this growing warmth and appearing to glow from within more intensely, the single falling drop acting as tiny lens concentrating light as it falls

SPATIAL LOGIC:
- FOREGROUND: Product bottle and hands at face height — the pour-action as hero detail. Sharp focus.
- MIDGROUND: Aira's face watching the pour, slightly soft (focus racking to product as hero).
- BACKGROUND: Dawn balcony with city skyline, brightening, morning mist, soft warm-cool.

LIGHTING: Dawn light progressing — warmer than Frame 1, more directional from left-horizon, product glass and liquid catching warmth increasingly. Cool-ambient diminishing. Light separation 1.5+ stops on product glass.

FRAMING: ECU on product-pour-action — product bottle and hands fill frame center, Aira's face visible in upper portion at slight soft-focus. Product-hero framing. Camera at product-level.

LENS: 100mm macro. APERTURE: f/2.8 — product and drop razor-sharp, face slightly soft, background very soft. Clean minimal bokeh.

COMPOSITION REFERENCE: Product-macro hero shot, single drop as focal point (Chanel beauty-film drop-shots), architectural precision.

ATMOSPHERE: The precision moment of product-meets-skin (about to happen), reverent care in application, dawn-light growing as metaphor for the foundation's illuminating effect. Minimal grain.

COLOR GRADE: Cool-warm transition progressing from Frame 1 — slightly more warm-gold on product now, skin still in cool-dominant environment but horizon-warmth growing. Product liquid as warmest element.

NEGATIVE: mirrored, flipped, inverted, extra limbs, fused fingers, melted features, asymmetric eyes (unintentional), garbled text, floating shadows, duplicated subjects, low-res patches, plastic skin, oversharpened, AI-generated artifacts, watermarks, signature, deformed hands, malformed teeth, joint cuts at ankle/knee/wrist/elbow/neck, amputated fingertips, cross-eyed, lazy eye, off-axis pupils, melted clothing, shoes-not-touching-ground, mismatched footwear pair, mannequin-stiff posture, dead eyes, statue-frozen energy, product label illegible, drop physics incorrect.

### Frame 4 — Reveal (Complete Glow)

FACIAL MICRO-DYNAMICS: Eyes — direct camera gaze (the only direct-address in this concept), calm and centered and GLOWING with the full-dawn-light now hitting her face, the confidence of beautiful skin, lashes natural but catching golden light. Foundation creating visible even glow across both cheekbones, catching morning light and holding it (the product-performance visible), contour natural from bone-structure only. Jaw — relaxed, soft. Breath — deep easy calm. The face of someone who knows she looks like dawn itself.

BODY POSTURE: Seated on balcony leaned back now (no longer leaning forward toward product — the action is complete), spine against chair back, open and relaxed, shoulders dropped, left shoulder still bare from shirt-fall. Comfortable and complete.

KINETIC STILLNESS — Six Layers:
1. Subject micro-action: Post-application stillness, the absolute calm of completion, only micro-breathing movement, the face as still canvas for light to play upon
2. Fabric/hair state: White shirt catching full morning warmth now with fabric translucency visible at thin areas, hair with morning-light-band warm and golden along straight lengths, breeze beginning to warm and move shirt-hem barely (morning air warming)
3. Particulate layer: Morning mist almost fully cleared, remaining 4-5 particles now caught in full warm-golden light (transformed from cool-blue mist of Frame 1 to warm-gold morning-air), dew on marble mostly evaporated leaving clean surface
4. Contact-point activity: Left hand resting on marble (now dry-warm vs wet-cool of Frame 1), body relaxed against chair back, shirt fabric resting on skin at off-shoulder point
5. Background motion: City skyline now clear and warm-lit (morning arrived), birds more active (several dots moving in sky), slight warm morning breeze establishing (shirt-hem micro-movement beginning)
6. Light in motion: FULL MORNING LIGHT — warm golden 4000K dominant from risen sun, cool-blue completely receded, product bottle on marble now acting as light-sculpture (honey-liquid glowing internally with full morning beam passing through, creating elaborate warm-caustic patterns on marble surface), Aira's face with foundation catching and holding morning light creating visible luminous-skin that seems to PRODUCE light rather than merely reflect it

- FOREGROUND: Product bottle on marble surface with elaborate warm caustic-refraction patterns radiating from it (the product-as-light-source metaphor). Beautiful light-play as product-hero-final-state. Lower 25%.
- MIDGROUND: Aira's luminous face in full morning light, sharp focus. The product-result visible on skin.
- BACKGROUND: City morning with clear skyline, warm-lit buildings, morning sky blue-gold. Soft focus, expansive, hopeful.

LIGHTING: Full morning sun from left (now risen above horizon), warm 4000K, beautiful directional with soft-cloud-diffusion, illuminating face and product fully. Fill from open sky at -1 stop. No rim needed (front-lit beauty-light for skin-hero). Light separation: skin luminosity 1.5+ stops above background due to foundation's light-catching properties.

FRAMING: Beauty portrait CU — top of head with 6% headroom to collarbone. Subject 75% of frame. Product visible in lower-foreground (establishing product-and-result connection). Camera at eye level. Direct-address composition.

COMPOSITION: Centered beauty-hero (Hoyte van Hoytema clean-centered, selective-warm), product in lower-third as grounding-object, face as upper-hero.

ATMOSPHERE: Morning arrived, warmth established, the product has done its work (bringing warmth and light to skin as dawn brought warmth and light to the balcony), reverent calm resolved into quiet confidence, the ritual complete. Minimal grain, polished.

COLOR GRADE: WARM ARRIVED — the full cool-to-warm arc of this concept resolved, golden morning dominant, skin GLOWING with selective warmth-enhancement (the foundation making skin read as the warmest most luminous element in frame), slight desaturation on background for skin-priority, cyan shadows gone (replaced by warm morning tones). The grade demonstrates the product-journey: from cool bare world to warm luminous completion.

NEGATIVE: mirrored, flipped, inverted, extra limbs, fused fingers, melted features, asymmetric eyes (unintentional), garbled text, floating shadows, duplicated subjects, low-res patches, plastic skin, oversharpened, AI-generated artifacts, watermarks, signature, deformed hands, malformed teeth, joint cuts at ankle/knee/wrist/elbow/neck, amputated fingertips, cross-eyed, lazy eye, off-axis pupils, melted clothing, shoes-not-touching-ground, mismatched footwear pair, mannequin-stiff posture, dead eyes, statue-frozen energy, product label illegible, skin appearing artificial.

## VIDEO PROMPTS

### Frame 1 — Video (Product Hover Hero)

SHOT TYPE: MS to CU (product-and-subject split-focus). CAMERA MOVEMENT: Slow push-in (from MS showing balcony setting to CU on product-hover over 3 seconds, smooth and deliberate). LENS: 85mm. SUBJECT ACTION: Aira seated on balcony at dawn, reaching toward hovering product. At 0.0s wide establishing (dawn balcony, city, her in white shirt), camera advancing. By 1.5s framing tightens to show product hovering with reflection on wet marble. At 2.0s her fingertips enter frame reaching toward bottle. At 2.5-3.0s fingers nearly touching but NOT contacting — the reverent-approach held. LIGHTING: 6AM cool-blue ambient with first warm-gold horizon-edge. Product glass glowing warm through honey-liquid in cool environment. ENVIRONMENT + ATMOSPHERE: Dawn balcony, marble surface with dew, city skyline in mist, cool morning air, slight visible breath-fog from cold, the product as warm-element in cool-world. AUDIO: Music: none (ambient-only concept — SILENT voice + minimal score). Ambient-only: distant city morning (far traffic hum barely audible, bird at 1.5s single chirp, wind very soft through balcony railing, the sound of dawn-quiet), slight wet-marble surface-reflection sound (nearly subliminal). Duration: 3 seconds. Frame rate: 24fps. Motion blur: 180-degree, minimal (slow push-in only). Temporal logic: 0.0-1.5s establishing push-in, 1.5-2.0s product-hover revealed, 2.0-3.0s fingertip-approach held.

NEGATIVE: morphing, warping, identity drift, limb teleport, object pop-in, frame skip, text overlay, watermark, AI artifact, ghosting, double exposure, unmotivated camera shake, physics violation, mannequin posture, frozen background, product-hover-breaking (must maintain float throughout), identity flicker.

### Frame 2 — Video (Pour/Application)

SHOT TYPE: ECU macro on product-pour. CAMERA MOVEMENT: Static macro-lock (product and drop as sole subjects in near-static frame). LENS: 100mm macro. SUBJECT ACTION: Pump depressed by finger, single drop emerging and falling in slow-motion toward waiting fingertip. At 0.0-1.0s pump depression visible, 1.0-2.0s drop forms at nozzle, 2.0-3.0s drop detaches and falls (caught in detail showing honey-golden liquid catching dawn-light mid-air). LIGHTING: Dawn light through product glass creating internal glow, drop catching light as individual tiny lens mid-fall. AUDIO: Ambient: pump-mechanism soft click at 0.5s, the near-silent sound of a single drop falling (micro-splash as it hits fingertip at 3.0s). Duration: 3 seconds. Frame rate: 24fps (drop-fall at real-time, not slow-motion — maintaining realism). Motion blur: drop-fall creating 2-frame natural blur trail. Temporal: 0.0-1.0s pump, 1.0-2.0s drop-forming, 2.0-3.0s drop-fall to fingertip.

NEGATIVE: [standard video negative], product-pour physics unrealistic, drop disappearing or multiplying.

### Frame 3 — Video (Blending)

SHOT TYPE: ECU face with application. CAMERA MOVEMENT: Slow push-in (from CU to ECU on cheekbone over 3 seconds, closing on the skin-transformation). LENS: 85mm. SUBJECT ACTION: Fingertip pat-pat-pat applying foundation to cheekbone in rhythmic gentle taps. Visible product blending and spreading across skin surface. Luminous-finish emerging where product is blended. Eyes half-closed in pleasure. The tactile beauty-ASMR moment. LIGHTING: Dawn warmth now on face, foundation creating visible light-catching-luminosity where blended. AUDIO: Ambient: fingertip-on-skin soft pats (3 per second rhythm, soft thuds), slight breath of pleasure from Aira (single exhale). Duration: 3 seconds. Frame rate: 24fps. Motion blur: fingertip-pat motion with slight blur between contacts. Temporal: continuous pat-pat-pat application over 3 seconds with visible skin-transformation-in-progress.

NEGATIVE: [standard video negative], skin transformation unrealistic, overly-quick product blending.

### Frame 4 — Video (Reveal)

SHOT TYPE: Beauty CU final. CAMERA MOVEMENT: Slow pull-back (ECU to CU over 3 seconds, revealing full luminous face in morning light — the final reveal). LENS: 85mm. SUBJECT ACTION: Application complete. Hands at rest. At 0.0s tight on skin-detail showing luminous finish. Pull-back reveals full face at 1.5s. At 2.0s eyes open fully to camera (the only direct-gaze of the concept). At 2.5s the smallest smile. At 3.0s held gaze with product visible in lower foreground (connection between product and result). LIGHTING: Full morning golden directional from left, skin GLOWING with foundation creating visible luminous-surface, beautiful and reverent. AUDIO: Ambient: morning birds (2-3 simultaneous now, slight melodic quality), gentle warm breeze, the sound of a morning fully arrived. Optional: single sustained piano note fading in at 2.0s and sustaining through (the only musical element in the entire concept — reverent and minimal). Duration: 3 seconds. Frame rate: 24fps. Motion blur: minimal (slow pull-back and face-stillness). Temporal: 0.0-1.5s skin-detail pull-back, 1.5-2.0s full face revealed, 2.0-3.0s direct-gaze and micro-smile held.

NEGATIVE: morphing, warping, identity drift, limb teleport, object pop-in, frame skip, text overlay, watermark, AI artifact, ghosting, double exposure, unmotivated camera shake, physics violation, mannequin posture, frozen background, identity flicker, product absent from frame in final reveal.

# CONCEPT 17 — BEAUTY AD

**Concept Line:** "What emerges when the surface breaks."
**Format:** Beauty Ad — Fragrance Mood Piece
**Product:** Perfume — faceted prism bottle, geometric multi-sided cut in deep midnight-blue glass, minimal label (single silver foil initial "A"), chrome weighted stopper shaped like a crescent, base facets refracting light into blue-violet spectrum on surfaces below, interior liquid: sheer violet-blue with suspended gold micro-particles
**Mood Archetype:** MA-14 "moon on glass"
**Sub-type:** Fragrance Mood Piece
**Duration:** 25 seconds total
**Frames:** 5 frames x 5 seconds each
**Register:** CONTEMPLATIVE
**Voice:** SILENT
**Product Move:** P-15 Liquid Mirror Emergence (product rises slowly from perfectly still water surface in a shallow black basin, surface tension holds until breach, water cascading down faceted surfaces)
**Camera:** Vertical tilt from water surface up to product apex, then pull-back to reveal Aira
**Setting:** B-7 Minimalist Gallery repurposed as midnight meditation space (black seamless backdrop, single overhead cool-white spot creating moon-like circle of light on floor, shallow obsidian basin with still water, slight fog rolling at floor level)
**Wardrobe:** Black silk column slip floor-length, invisible straps, fabric absorbing light
**Hair:** HC-9 Slicked-Back Wet — modern futurist, fully pulled back exposing full face and neck
**Makeup:** ML-28 Wet-Look Skin — extreme glossy skin, no powder, defined eye with silver inner-corner
**Color Grade:** Desaturated near-monochrome, deep blue-black shadows, selective silver highlights on product facets and skin highlights only, crushed deep blacks, A24-meets-Greig Fraser (Dune blue-silver palette)

## IMAGE PROMPTS

### Frame 1 — Water Surface (Pre-Emergence)

ASPECT RATIO: 9:16 vertical. SUBJECT: AIRA — Adult woman late 20s-early 30s, South Asian (Indian), warm honey-to-caramel skin tone with golden undertone, 5'6"-5'8", soft-strong hourglass-athletic silhouette, fuller sculpted legs with toned thigh definition, fuller shapely thighs, fuller feminine arms with subtle muscle tone, fuller defined chest in proportion, flat toned midsection, defined waist clear waist-to-hip ratio, curvy hip line with natural feminine flare, heart-shaped to oval face, defined cheekbones, full defined lips with natural cupid's bow, almond-shaped expressive eyes dark brown iris with subtle amber flecks, strong but feminine groomed naturally arched brow, natural sun-kissed glow, long dark brown to near-black hair with subtle warm highlights naturally textured soft waves with body and movement, elegant well-groomed hands.

PRODUCT: Perfume bottle — NOT YET VISIBLE in this frame. Only the still water surface of the shallow obsidian basin visible, perfectly mirror-flat. The product is BELOW the surface (about to emerge in subsequent frames). The water surface shows a slight disturbance beginning at center — concentric micro-ripples suggesting something approaching from below. Chrome crescent-stopper creating the first break-point: its tip is just barely visible at water-surface-level (1mm above), the first emergence.

WARDROBE STATE: Black silk column slip floor-length (the dress absorbs light, creating a negative-space silhouette effect against the black backdrop — she is defined by the moonlight-spot rather than by contrast with background). Invisible straps, fabric falling straight from chest to floor without gathering. Standing at edge of the obsidian basin.

HAIR STATE: HC-9 Slicked-Back Wet — hair fully pulled back from face with gel-wet finish, slicked flat to skull exposing full face architecture, ears, neck, jawline completely visible. Hair gathered at nape in a slick flat continuation (not a bun — just slicked back into a flat-against-head stream). Modern futurist, the most stripped-back hair possible to expose the face and product interaction.

MAKEUP STATE: ML-28 Wet-Look Skin — extreme glossy skin (applied oil/gloss product creating reflective-wet surface appearance on forehead, cheekbones, nose bridge, chin), no powder at all, defined eye with dark precise lid-liner and silver inner-corner highlight (the only point of sparkle on her face — echoing the silver/chrome of the product). No visible base (the wet-look IS the look). Dark defined lash. Bare lip with slight natural color and gloss.

HAND POSITIONS: Right hand extended over the basin surface, palm-down, hovering 10cm above the water. Fingers slightly spread as if sensing the energy of what is about to emerge below. Left hand at her side, pressed flat against the silk slip at her thigh (grounding). The reaching-hand as invitation or summoning gesture over the water.

FACIAL MICRO-DYNAMICS: Eyes — looking down at the water surface (watching the first micro-ripples and crescent-tip emergence), heavy-lidded and contemplative (the mood archetype: "moon on glass" — still, reflective, lunar), wet-look-skin catching the single overhead spotlight creating visible reflection-points on forehead and nose bridge, silver inner-corner catching light as a single star-point in the otherwise dark-palette face. Brows — relaxed and minimal, the expression of watching and waiting. Lips — slightly parted on slow breath, wet-glossy natural color, no tension (contemplative peace). Cheeks — extreme wet-look creating visible light-pools on cheekbone peaks (almost liquid-appearing). Jaw — relaxed, dropped slightly, throat exposed and elongated by the slicked-back hair (full neck architecture visible). Breath — deep slow rhythmic (meditative), body still.

BODY POSTURE: Standing at basin edge, weight evenly distributed, spine elongated and straight, shoulders back revealing full neck and collarbone line (enhanced by invisible straps and slicked hair), right arm extended over basin with hovering hand, left arm at side. Tall and still. The posture of someone in ceremony.

KINETIC STILLNESS — Six Layers:
1. Subject micro-action: Right hand hovering motionless over water, the sensing-gesture, slight finger-spread micro-tremor (energy awareness), eyes tracking the first emergence-tip below
2. Fabric/hair state: Black silk column slip hanging straight with gravitational weight, zero movement (still air in gallery space), slicked-wet-hair with gel-sealed zero-movement (frozen-liquid effect against skull), fabric absorbing all light creating pure-silhouette quality
3. Particulate layer: Floor-level fog rolling slowly inward from edges of frame (theatrical fog machine at ground-level), 20+ fog particles visible in the overhead spotlight beam, creating moon-like atmosphere. Fog hugging floor and basin base without reaching water surface
4. Contact-point activity: Left hand pressing flat against silk-on-thigh (slight fabric-indent), feet on floor (bare? or invisible-black flat shoes) with grounded full-contact weight, right hand hovering without contact (the anticipation-of-contact)
5. Background motion: Floor fog rolling slowly inward from all edges (radial inward drift, 2cm/s), slight fog-eddy around her feet and basin base, otherwise total stillness of the black seamless space
6. Light in motion: Single overhead cool-white spot creating hard-edged circle of light on floor (moon-circle, 2m diameter), Aira and basin both within this circle, fog catching the moon-spot-edge and creating visible atmospheric edge-glow, water surface with the emerging crescent-tip creating first micro-ripple-reflection of overhead light (concentric light-rings on the dark water)

SPATIAL LOGIC:
- FOREGROUND: Obsidian basin (shallow, matte-black stone or ceramic, 60cm diameter) with still water showing first concentric ripples from crescent-tip emergence. Micro-reflections of overhead spot on water surface. Sharp focus hero-element.
- MIDGROUND: Aira standing at basin edge, sharp focus, wet-look-skin catching moon-spot, contemplative-ceremony posture.
- BACKGROUND: Black seamless backdrop — pure negative space. No detail, no texture, just absorption. The product and subject exist in a void defined only by the overhead moon-spot light-circle and floor fog.

LIGHTING:
- Key: Single overhead cool-white spot (6500K, hard-edged circular beam from directly above), creating "moon" effect — hard pool of light on floor containing Aira and basin, everything outside the circle in near-total black
- Fill: NONE (the black-void is intentional, shadow-side is pure dark)
- Rim: Slight overhead-spot edge catching her shoulder-line and slicked-hair-crown (the spot is directly above, creating downward-lit top-rim)
- Practical: Water-surface micro-reflections bouncing moon-spot upward onto underside of Aira's hovering hand (the water as practical reflector)
- Light separation: 3+ stops between lit-circle and surrounding black void (extreme contrast)

FRAMING: Full-body in context — top of head with 10% headroom to feet with fog visible. Subject 45% of frame height. Camera at waist-level. Body angle: profile-to-3/4, basin visible in front of her, reaching arm extended over it. Wide enough to show the ceremony-context: her, the basin, the moon-circle, the fog, the void.

LENS: 50mm. APERTURE: f/2.8 — subject and basin sharp, fog at edges soft, pure black background (no bokeh needed — no elements to blur, just void).

COMPOSITION REFERENCE: A24 atmospheric minimalism (Under the Skin void-room reference), Greig Fraser Dune ceremonial-lighting, single-source-dramatic, the void as composition-element.

ATMOSPHERE: Midnight meditation, lunar ceremony, water as mirror-portal, the product about to emerge from the depths, fog as mystery-atmosphere, the gallery-void as sacred space. Zero grain (polished, cinematic, clean).

COLOR GRADE: Near-monochrome blue-silver — DEEP blue-black shadows (crushed), selective SILVER on highlights only (skin wet-points, water-reflections, crescent-tip chrome), mid-tones nearly absent (high-contrast with very little middle-ground), slight violet undertone in the deepest shadows. Greig Fraser Dune blue-silver palette. Skin reads as warm-ONLY by contrast with the extreme cool environment.

NEGATIVE: mirrored, flipped, inverted, extra limbs, fused fingers, melted features, asymmetric eyes (unintentional), garbled text, floating shadows, duplicated subjects, low-res patches, plastic skin, oversharpened, AI-generated artifacts, watermarks, signature, deformed hands, malformed teeth, joint cuts at ankle/knee/wrist/elbow/neck, amputated fingertips, cross-eyed, lazy eye, off-axis pupils, melted clothing, shoes-not-touching-ground, mismatched footwear pair, mannequin-stiff posture, dead eyes, statue-frozen energy, fog above waist-level (must stay floor-level), water surface not perfectly still (must show mirror-quality until emergence-ripple), crescent-tip not visible at surface.

### Frame 2 — Emergence (Product Rising)

ASPECT RATIO: 9:16 vertical. SUBJECT: AIRA — [full identity lock]. PRODUCT: Perfume bottle NOW EMERGING from water — risen to 50% visibility above surface. Water cascading down the geometric faceted midnight-blue glass surfaces, individual water-streams following the facet-edges and dripping from vertices. Chrome crescent stopper fully above water, catching overhead moon-spot with bright silver-reflection. Facets below water still visible through refraction (distorted geometry beneath surface). Water surface tension broken with concentric ripple-rings radiating from emergence-point across basin surface. Blue-violet light refractions from facets beginning to cast onto water surface and basin rim.

All other elements (wardrobe, hair, makeup, posture) unchanged from Frame 1 except: Aira's right hand has moved CLOSER — now 3cm above the bottle's crescent stopper, nearly touching (the magnetic approach). Her expression shifts from watching-the-water to watching-the-emerged-product with intensified fascination (eyes wider, lips slightly more parted, the intake-breath of seeing it break surface).

KINETIC STILLNESS layers adjusted for: water actively cascading down product facets (kinetic water on still glass), concentric ripples actively expanding outward on basin surface (wave-motion radiating), product at the apex of its rise (hovering at 50% emergence, neither rising nor falling — frozen at peak).

LIGHTING adjusted for: product facets now catching and refracting the overhead moon-spot, creating new blue-violet caustic-projections on water surface and basin rim and Aira's hovering hand (the product CREATES light-patterns as it emerges).

FRAMING: Tighter than Frame 1 — MCU on product-and-Aira's-face composition. Product at center-frame emerging from water, Aira's face in upper portion looking down at it, her hand between product and her face. Camera at water-surface-level (dramatic low-angle showing emergence).

All other specifications (lens, aperture, composition reference, atmosphere, color grade, negative) as Frame 1 with the addition of: water-physics must be realistic (cascading following gravity, surface-tension ripples expanding at correct speed), product emergence must appear gravitationally impossible but visually convincing (as if rising by its own will).

### Frame 3 — Full Reveal (Product Ascended)

ASPECT RATIO: 9:16 vertical. SUBJECT: AIRA — [full identity lock]. PRODUCT: Fully emerged and hovering 5cm above water surface. All water has cascaded off (facets now dry and catching light with full intensity). Geometric midnight-blue glass refracting overhead moonlight into elaborate blue-violet spectrum patterns on all surfaces below and around it. Chrome crescent stopper reflecting the overhead spot as a bright star-point. The product at its most powerful and sculptural — fully revealed.

Aira's right hand now at the product's height but still not touching — 2cm away. Fingertips parallel to bottle body creating energy-field-tension between skin and glass. Her expression: full contemplative wonder, the "moon on glass" mood fully embodied. Eyes level with product. Silver inner-corner highlight echoing the chrome crescent. Wet-look skin catching ALL the blue-violet refractions from the product's facets — her face is painted in the product's light-language.

FRAMING: MCU balanced — product and face at same height sharing frame-center, both sharp, the product's light-patterns visible ON her skin (connection between product and person literal through light).

LIGHTING: Overhead moon-spot plus now the PRODUCT as secondary light-source (refracting overhead beam into violet-blue patterns that illuminate surfaces around it). Two-source-effect: primary overhead + product-refracted-secondary.

### Frame 4 — Connection (Perfume Applied)

ASPECT RATIO: 9:16 vertical. SUBJECT: AIRA — [full identity lock]. PRODUCT: Now held in right hand (she finally made contact — took it from its hover). Pressed against her left wrist in the classic perfume-application-pose. A single spray visible as ultra-fine mist between nozzle and wrist (the crescent-stopper removed revealing spray mechanism). Mist catching overhead spotlight with prismatic quality.

MAKEUP/SKIN: Wet-look unchanged, but the blue-violet light-refractions from the bottle now closer to her face and more intimate (held at wrist, patterns falling on inner arm and jaw from close proximity).

HAND POSITIONS: Right hand holding bottle at left wrist, pressing spray. Left wrist presented upward, inner arm exposed (pulse-point targeting). The classic intimate fragrance-application gesture.

FACIAL MICRO-DYNAMICS: Eyes — closed (the sensory-moment of smelling fragrance, the private enjoyment), lashes creating crescents on cheeks, the expression of pure olfactory pleasure. Slight head-tilt toward wrist (leaning into the scent). Lips pressed together in pleasure-smile.

FRAMING: ECU — face and wrist-application intimate. Spray mist visible between bottle and skin.

### Frame 5 — Aftermath (Contemplative Hold)

ASPECT RATIO: 9:16 vertical. SUBJECT: AIRA — [full identity lock]. PRODUCT: Set beside the obsidian basin on the floor, standing upright, crescent-stopper replaced. At rest in its final position, facets still catching and refracting moon-spot into blue-violet patterns on the wet basin rim and floor-fog around it. The product as sculpture-at-rest.

Aira: Stepped back from basin, now in full-body visibility. One arm crossed over chest holding opposite bicep (the self-embrace pose of someone in a contemplative after-moment). Head slightly tilted down, eyes looking at the product from distance. The separation after intimacy. The mood fully realized.

FRAMING: Wide — full body + product + basin + fog + void. The complete scene as final tableau. Camera pulling back to reveal the midnight-meditation-space in full. The relationship between person and product established across space.

LIGHTING: Overhead moon-spot containing both Aira and product-at-basin within its circle, fog rolling at edges, the completed ceremony-space visible. Blue-violet refractions from product creating final light-patterns in the fog at floor level.

COLOR GRADE: Peak blue-silver desaturation. Near-monochrome completed. The most visually extreme of all concepts — A24 meets Greig Fraser at maximum artistic-expression. Silver ONLY on product chrome and skin wet-highlights. Everything else crushed to deep blue-black.

Duration: 5 seconds. Frame rate: 24fps. Motion blur: spray-mist with slight diffusion.

# CONCEPT 18 — BEAUTY AD

**Concept Line:** "Every shade is a story waiting to be told."
**Format:** Beauty Ad — Product Launch
**Product:** Eyeshadow palette — sculptural clamshell form in matte black ceramic with gold-leaf interior hinge visible when open, 9 pans in warm-to-cool gradient (champagne, rose-gold, burnt sienna, terracotta, plum, deep olive, navy, charcoal, matte black), each pan pressed with subtle geometric texture pattern, magnetic closure with satisfying snap, compact-mirror inside lid
**Mood Archetype:** MA-25 "hand-thrown clay still warm"
**Sub-type:** Product Launch Ad
**Duration:** 24 seconds total
**Frames:** 6 frames x 4 seconds each
**Register:** KNOWING
**Voice:** SELECTIVE — single line "Nine stories. One palette." delivered at frame 4
**Product Move:** P-14 Bloom Reveal (palette opens slowly from closed to full 180-degree flat, panels unfolding with mechanical precision)
**Camera:** Macro push-in on palette surface + orbit quarter-turn around product
**Setting:** B-5 Atelier / Workshop (wooden workbench surface with natural grain, clay pots with brushes, large north-facing window with cool natural daylight, slight dust in beam, artisan aesthetic)
**Wardrobe:** Cream oversized linen shirt sleeves rolled to elbow, silver delicate bracelet L wrist
**Hair:** HC-25 Morning Coffee Wave — second-day texture, soft at temples
**Makeup:** ML-20 Bronze-Glow Sun — bronze cheek, gold eyelid (demonstrating palette shades), nude lip
**Color Grade:** Warm daylight with slight desaturation on background, skin-priority warm, artisan matte feel, subtle grain, warm highlights on product gold-leaf

## IMAGE PROMPTS

### Frame 1 — Product Closed (Object Design)

ASPECT RATIO: 9:16 vertical. SUBJECT: AIRA — Adult woman late 20s-early 30s, South Asian (Indian), warm honey-to-caramel skin tone with golden undertone, 5'6"-5'8", soft-strong hourglass-athletic silhouette, fuller sculpted legs with toned thigh definition, fuller shapely thighs, fuller feminine arms with subtle muscle tone, fuller defined chest in proportion, flat toned midsection, defined waist clear waist-to-hip ratio, curvy hip line with natural feminine flare, heart-shaped to oval face, defined cheekbones, full defined lips with natural cupid's bow, almond-shaped expressive eyes dark brown iris with subtle amber flecks, strong but feminine groomed naturally arched brow, natural sun-kissed glow, long dark brown to near-black hair with subtle warm highlights naturally textured soft waves with body and movement, elegant well-groomed hands.

PRODUCT: Eyeshadow palette CLOSED — sculptural matte black ceramic clamshell resting on wooden workbench surface. Visible: matte-black exterior with subtle curved form (clamshell shape), gold-leaf hinge visible at back edge catching north-light with warm metallic glow, magnetic-closure seam visible as a precise line around the perimeter, the ceramic material with slight handmade-texture visible at macro level. The palette as OBJECT first — beautiful before even opened.

WARDROBE STATE: Cream oversized linen shirt (natural texture visible, slightly wrinkled from being lived-in), sleeves rolled to elbow revealing forearms and silver delicate bracelet on left wrist. Sitting at the workbench implying artisan-creative context.

HAIR STATE: HC-25 Morning Coffee Wave — second-day texture (not freshly washed, slight natural oils giving body), soft at temples with pieces falling forward, overall loose and natural with gentle undone-wave. Warm-toned.

MAKEUP STATE: ML-20 Bronze-Glow Sun — warm bronze on cheekbones (demonstrating palette's warmer shades), gold shimmer on eyelids (champagne from palette visible on skin), nude natural lip, defined brow, glowing warm skin. She is wearing the palette's story on her face.

Left hand resting on workbench surface, silver bracelet visible, fingers relaxed near clay pots with brushes.

FACIAL MICRO-DYNAMICS: Eyes — looking at the closed palette with knowing appreciation (she knows what is inside — the knowing register), slight downcast gaze at the product, gold shimmer on lids visible and catching north-light through window, the expression of someone about to share a secret. Brows — one lifted slightly (the knowing tease — "wait until you see"). Lips — soft knowing half-smile, closed-lip (the pre-reveal expression), nude color warm. Cheeks — bronze visible on bone-peaks catching natural window light. Jaw — relaxed and confident. Breath — held in anticipation of the reveal.

BODY POSTURE: Seated at wooden workbench (high stool, artisan workspace), torso forward-leaned toward product on bench surface, elbows on table, intimate with the object. Artisan-creative posture — she is the maker-revealer not just the wearer.

KINETIC STILLNESS — Six Layers:
1. Subject micro-action: Right hand resting on palette with thumb micro-tracing the ceramic surface texture (tactile appreciation), the about-to-open anticipation in the finger-placement at opening-edge
2. Fabric/hair state: Cream linen shirt with soft wrinkles catching varied depths of north-light at sleeve-rolls, morning coffee wave with temple-pieces falling forward creating soft face-frame, slight movement from her forward-lean breath
3. Particulate layer: North-facing window natural daylight creating visible dust-beam crossing the workbench at an angle (the atelier atmosphere), 15-20 particles in the beam moving slowly in gentle air-current, some catching light as warm (reflecting off gold-leaf hinge) while most read cool (direct daylight)
4. Contact-point activity: Right palm curved over ceramic palette surface with finger-pressure visible, right fingertips at seam-edge ready to open, left fingers on rough wooden bench surface (texture-contact with rustic wood grain), silver bracelet links pressing into wrist
5. Background motion: Atelier space — dust slowly drifting in north-light beam, slight shadow-movement on back wall from exterior tree outside north-facing window, clay pots with brushes completely still, the slow organic pace of a creative workspace
6. Light in motion: North-facing window providing steady directional cool-daylight (the classic artist's light — consistent and true), slight warmth introduced only by the gold-leaf hinge reflecting north-light back as warm-metallic-bounce onto nearby surfaces, dust particles drifting through the beam creating slow-moving light-scatter

SPATIAL LOGIC:
- FOREGROUND: Wooden workbench surface with natural grain visible, palette as central object, clay pots with brushes beside it, a few loose pigment-powders scattered on bench surface (artisan-context). Product as hero center-foreground.
- MIDGROUND: Aira seated at bench, hands on product, sharp focus, the knowing-revealer.
- BACKGROUND: Atelier — large north-facing window (industrial-size, multi-paned), cool natural daylight streaming, visible dust-beam, wooden shelving with ceramic objects and art supplies, white-washed brick wall. Artisan aesthetic. Soft focus with grain.

LIGHTING:
- Key: North-facing window natural daylight from camera-left, cool 5500K, soft and even (directional but not hard — the classic north-light for color-accuracy), the "artist's light" providing true-color on product surfaces
- Fill: Room ambient from white-washed walls at -1.5 stops, soft and neutral
- Rim: None (natural single-source simplicity)
- Practical: None (pure natural daylight)
- Light separation: Product and hands 1.5+ stops above background due to proximity to window (inverse square law)

FRAMING: MCU with product hero — product at center-lower-frame on bench surface, Aira's face and torso in upper portion leaning toward it. Both product and subject share frame. Camera at bench-surface-level (product-elevation angle, slightly looking up at Aira). Split attention between object-design and human-reaction.

LENS: 85mm portrait-macro hybrid. APERTURE: f/2.8 — product AND hands sharp (same focal plane), face sharp, background atelier soft with warm-tone grain.

COMPOSITION REFERENCE: Product-hero with artisan context (Byredo campaign aesthetic), natural-light workshop photography (Irving Penn still-life approach adapted), warm-earthen palette.

ATMOSPHERE: Artisan workshop warmth, handcrafted-object appreciation, north-light-as-truth (the color-accuracy light for the color-product), the palette as art-object before cosmetic-tool, maker-revealer energy. Slight film grain (artisan warmth).

COLOR GRADE: Warm daylight with artisan-matte quality — wood tones warm and rich, ceramic matte-black reading as warm-neutral (not cold), gold-leaf as warmest metallic accent, skin bronze-warm-prioritized, background slightly desaturated to push product and skin forward. Subtle grain throughout for tactile-analog quality. Warm highlights, cool-neutral shadows from north-light.

NEGATIVE: mirrored, flipped, inverted, extra limbs, fused fingers, melted features, asymmetric eyes (unintentional), garbled text, floating shadows, duplicated subjects, low-res patches, plastic skin, oversharpened, AI-generated artifacts, watermarks, signature, deformed hands, malformed teeth, joint cuts at ankle/knee/wrist/elbow/neck, amputated fingertips, cross-eyed, lazy eye, off-axis pupils, melted clothing, shoes-not-touching-ground, mismatched footwear pair, mannequin-stiff posture, dead eyes, statue-frozen energy, palette surface texture not visible, gold-leaf not catching light.

ASPECT RATIO: 9:16 vertical. SUBJECT: AIRA — [full identity lock]. PRODUCT: Palette MID-OPEN — captured at 90-degree angle (half-open, lid rising like a wing), interior NOW VISIBLE: gold-leaf interior hinge catching north-light with full metallic glow, 9 pans in warm-to-cool gradient becoming visible (champagne catching most light at the opened-edge, darker shades in shadow at the still-partially-hidden far-edge). Each pan's geometric pressed-texture visible at the opened angle. Compact-mirror inside lid reflecting the north-light downward onto the pans (creating secondary illumination on the pigments). Magnetic closure released — the precise moment after the snap-open (satisfying mechanical precision implied).

FACIAL MICRO-DYNAMICS: Eyes now directed at the interior being revealed (watching the pans appear as lid rises), slight widening with the pleasure of revealing something beautiful, gold shimmer on her own lids echoing the champagne pan being revealed, knowing-smile deepening.

# CONCEPT 19 — BEAUTY AD

**Concept Line:** "One drop. Everything changes."
**Format:** Beauty Ad — Sensory Beauty Tutorial
**Product:** Liquid highlighter — apothecary-style amber glass dropper bottle, hand-applied cream paper label with hand-lettered "GLOW" in copper ink, ceramic dropper bulb in natural stoneware color, golden-champagne liquid visible inside with micro-shimmer suspended, cork accent ring at neck
**Mood Archetype:** MA-21 "fingertip at the inner wrist"
**Sub-type:** Sensory Beauty Tutorial
**Duration:** 20 seconds total
**Frames:** 5 frames x 4 seconds each
**Register:** TENDER
**Voice:** SPOKEN — intimate tutorial "One drop here... blend with warmth... bas, dekhlo."
**Product Move:** P-7 Gravity-Free Pour (single drop exits dropper but instead of falling, curves in a gentle arc mid-air before landing on fingertip — restrained, one impossible moment)
**Camera:** ECU push-in on cheekbone application moment
**Setting:** B-4 Dawn Balcony (cool 7AM light, dew on railing, soft city below in fog, cool-warm transition on skin)
**Wardrobe:** Soft grey cashmere wrap cardigan, bare collarbone exposed
**Hair:** HC-23 Air-Dried Boho — natural undone morning texture
**Makeup:** ML-1 Bare-Glow — dewy nothing, tinted balm only (the highlighter IS the tutorial subject, applied during reel)
**Color Grade:** Soft cool-warm transition, morning fresh, skin priority, slight blue in shadows transitioning to gold where light hits skin, Lubezki natural-light-worship reference

## IMAGE PROMPTS

### Frame 1 — Product Introduction

ASPECT RATIO: 9:16 vertical. SUBJECT: AIRA — Adult woman late 20s-early 30s, South Asian (Indian), warm honey-to-caramel skin tone with golden undertone, 5'6"-5'8", soft-strong hourglass-athletic silhouette, fuller sculpted legs with toned thigh definition, fuller shapely thighs, fuller feminine arms with subtle muscle tone, fuller defined chest in proportion, flat toned midsection, defined waist clear waist-to-hip ratio, curvy hip line with natural feminine flare, heart-shaped to oval face, defined cheekbones, full defined lips with natural cupid's bow, almond-shaped expressive eyes dark brown iris with subtle amber flecks, strong but feminine groomed naturally arched brow, natural sun-kissed glow, long dark brown to near-black hair with subtle warm highlights naturally textured soft waves with body and movement, elegant well-groomed hands.

PRODUCT: Liquid highlighter bottle held in left hand at face-height — amber glass catching 7AM light with warm internal glow, cream paper label with "GLOW" in copper hand-lettering visible, ceramic dropper bulb in natural stoneware color (organic-artisanal), golden-champagne liquid visible through amber glass with suspended micro-shimmer catching light as individual tiny glint-points, cork accent ring at neck providing warm natural-material-accent. The product is BEAUTIFUL as object — apothecary charm meets clean beauty.

WARDROBE STATE: Soft grey cashmere wrap cardigan, loosely draped over shoulders, open at front revealing bare collarbones and upper chest. Soft texture catching 7AM cool light with slight fuzz-halo at edges. Morning-comfort-luxe.

HAIR STATE: HC-23 Air-Dried Boho — natural morning texture, undone and beautiful, slight overnight-wave from sleep without effort, no product, no styling. Falling naturally with some pieces at face and some behind shoulders. Real morning hair.

MAKEUP STATE: ML-1 Bare-Glow — dewy nothing visible. Only tinted lip balm (soft peach-pink). Natural skin with slight natural morning-radiance but no product (the highlighter IS the tutorial — she is starting bare so the effect is visible).

HAND POSITIONS: Left hand holding the amber dropper bottle at face-height beside her right cheek, presenting it to camera. Right hand reaching up with dropper pulled from bottle — ceramic bulb between thumb and index, glass dropper tube visible with a single golden-champagne drop forming at the tip (about to demonstrate). Intimate tutorial-hand-gesture proximity.

FACIAL MICRO-DYNAMICS: Eyes — direct soft gaze to camera (the tutorial-address, intimate and instructional), gentle and inviting, the expression of sharing a secret with a close friend, catchlight at 3 o'clock from 7AM dawn-light (cool with first warm edges). Brows — soft and natural, slightly raised in the "watch this" expression (inviting attention). Lips — tinted balm with slight smile at 40% (tender, sharing), the lips of someone about to speak intimately. Cheeks — completely bare (no highlighter yet — the "before" state clearly visible, natural cheekbone definition without product enhancement). Jaw — relaxed and soft, chin slightly forward (presenting/teaching posture). Breath — easy natural, the calm of a morning tutorial moment.

BODY POSTURE: Seated on balcony chair (modern minimal), wrapped in cashmere cardigan, morning-comfort, leaned slightly toward camera (teaching-lean), both arms raised with product and dropper at face-height. Bare collarbone exposed between cardigan folds. Relaxed morning posture with slight instructional forward-lean.

KINETIC STILLNESS — Six Layers:
1. Subject micro-action: Golden drop forming at dropper-tube-tip (about to exit — the surface-tension-moment before the gravity-free pour), right hand holding dropper steady with tutorial-precision, slight teaching-forward-lean
2. Fabric/hair state: Cashmere cardigan soft and draping with fuzzy-edge-halo catching cool morning backlight, air-dried hair with natural morning movement in dawn-breeze (slight strand lift at right temple)
3. Particulate layer: Cool 7AM morning air with slight visible mist/moisture in atmosphere, dew visible on balcony railing behind her, 8-10 ultra-fine morning-mist particles in cool light between camera and subject, the morning-fresh-air-quality visible
4. Contact-point activity: Left fingers on amber glass bottle (warm glass from liquid inside, slight condensation on cool exterior from morning temperature), right thumb and index pressing ceramic dropper-bulb, golden drop at tube-tip surface-tension-bond to glass
5. Background motion: Soft city below in morning fog — distant buildings barely visible through mist, slight fog-drift at mid-distance, dew on metal balcony railing with one droplet slowly moving along rail (gravity-descent in morning cool)
6. Light in motion: 7AM cool-warm transition — dominant cool 6500K ambient with warm 3500K beginning at horizon from rising sun, creating color-temperature gradient across frame (cool from above and sides, warm growing from camera-left-low), amber bottle glass acting as warm-filter catching and holding the first warm rays while surrounding air remains cool

SPATIAL LOGIC:
- FOREGROUND: Product bottle and dropper at face-height as primary hero (she is presenting it to camera). Sharp focus. Center-frame.
- MIDGROUND: Aira's face as tutorial-host and eventual-application-canvas. Sharp focus.
- BACKGROUND: Dawn balcony — railing with dew, soft foggy city below, cool morning sky with warm-horizon-edge, minimal and airy. Very soft focus.

LIGHTING:
- Key: 7AM natural daylight, cool-dominant 6500K with warm-edge growing from horizon-left (3500K first rays), soft and directional, the classic cool-morning-light-worship
- Fill: Sky-ambient from above at -0.5 stops (open-sky balcony)
- Rim: First warm-ray from horizon creating thin warm-gold edge on left side of product glass and left cheekbone (the product-and-skin catching the same warm light — CONNECTION)
- Practical: Amber glass bottle glowing warm internally (liquid catching warm-ray through amber filter creating golden internal glow)
- Light separation: Product bottle 1.5+ stops brighter than background (amber glass concentrating warm light while environment remains cool)

FRAMING: MCU tutorial frame — product at center, face beside/behind, both in sharp focus. Camera at face-level. Direct-address tutorial composition (intimate, close, teaching). Subject 65% of frame with product as co-hero.

LENS: 85mm. APERTURE: f/2.0 — product and face sharp (similar distance), background balcony dissolved to cool-morning bokeh.

COMPOSITION REFERENCE: Tutorial-intimate (beauty YouTube/TikTok framing elevated to cinematic quality), Lubezki natural-light-worship within the product-demonstration format, skin-as-canvas centered.

ATMOSPHERE: Dawn balcony fresh morning, the specific intimacy of a one-on-one beauty tutorial at dawn, sharing a secret product, cool morning air with warm light arriving, dew and mist and softness. Minimal grain (clean-beauty-tutorial aesthetic).

COLOR GRADE: Cool-warm transition — blue-cool shadows and environment, warm-gold ONLY where first-light hits (product glass, skin highlights, horizon-edge), the grade itself demonstrating the product's promise (it brings warmth/glow to cool skin). Lubezki reference: natural desaturated cool with selective warm pop where light touches. Skin-priority-warm at contact-points.

NEGATIVE: mirrored, flipped, inverted, extra limbs, fused fingers, melted features, asymmetric eyes (unintentional), garbled text, floating shadows, duplicated subjects, low-res patches, plastic skin, oversharpened, AI-generated artifacts, watermarks, signature, deformed hands, malformed teeth, joint cuts at ankle/knee/wrist/elbow/neck, amputated fingertips, cross-eyed, lazy eye, off-axis pupils, melted clothing, shoes-not-touching-ground, mismatched footwear pair, mannequin-stiff posture, dead eyes, statue-frozen energy, product label illegible, dropper-physics unrealistic.

### Frame 2 — Gravity-Free Pour (Product Move)

ASPECT RATIO: 9:16 vertical. SUBJECT: AIRA — [full identity lock]. PRODUCT MOVE: The single impossible moment — golden-champagne drop has exited the dropper tube and instead of falling straight down, CURVES in a gentle arc mid-air (as if guided by invisible force) before landing on Aira's presented fingertip. The drop caught mid-arc — visible as a perfect golden sphere suspended in air at the apex of its curve, catching morning light and appearing to glow internally from the shimmer-particles inside it. The ONE impossible-moment that defines this product-move. Restrained, singular, poetic.

HAND POSITIONS: Right hand still holding dropper (slightly above and to the left), the drop having just exited. Left hand positioned below and to the right, index fingertip presented upward as the landing-target. The drop mid-arc between the two — the spatial relationship showing the impossible curve-path clearly.

FACIAL MICRO-DYNAMICS: Eyes — tracking the drop's arc with subtle wonder (not shock — gentle fascination, as if this is the most natural thing in the world), gaze following the golden sphere mid-flight. The tender-wonder of the tutorial-host sharing something special. All other expressions soft and present.

FRAMING: ECU on the drop-in-arc — the drop itself as the HERO of this frame. Hands visible (source-dropper and destination-fingertip), face slightly softer in background but present. The impossible-moment as visual centerpiece.

LENS: 100mm macro. APERTURE: f/2.0 — drop razor-sharp (even individual shimmer-particles inside it visible as tiny glint-points), hands slightly softer, face as context.

### Frame 3 — Application (Cheekbone Touch)

ASPECT RATIO: 9:16 vertical. SUBJECT: AIRA — [full identity lock]. PRODUCT: Drop now on fingertip. Fingertip pressing into LEFT cheekbone with the golden-champagne liquid (application moment). Visible at point-of-contact: golden product on skin creating immediate visible glow-effect at the touch-point, blending outward from center with the warmth of her skin activating the shimmer.

HAND POSITIONS: Right hand at left cheekbone, index fingertip pressing golden product into skin in slow circular motion (visible product on finger AND on skin at contact-point). Left hand holding bottle in lap or at chest (secondary, soft focus).

MAKEUP STATE CHANGING: Left cheekbone now showing visible highlighter at application-point — a golden-champagne glow-spot where fingertip presses, radiating outward in a 3cm circle of increasing-luminosity (the product-effect visible in real-time formation on skin).

FACIAL MICRO-DYNAMICS: Eyes — slightly closed in the sensory pleasure of application (the feel of product on skin, fingertip warmth blending), tutorial-intimacy of the shared-sensory-moment. Lips forming the tutorial-words ("One drop here..."). Cheeks — LEFT cheekbone showing the product-glow-formation-in-progress (the hero-detail), RIGHT cheekbone bare for comparison.

FRAMING: ECU on cheekbone application — extreme close on skin-level showing texture and product interaction. The macro-beauty-tutorial-moment.

### Frame 4 — Blend (Warmth Activation)

ASPECT RATIO: 9:16 vertical. SUBJECT: AIRA — [full identity lock]. APPLICATION PROGRESS: Both cheekbones now showing golden-champagne highlighter fully blended.
