The before/after visible: bare forehead vs. glowing cheekbones.

HAND POSITIONS: Hands lowering after application (complete), right hand dropping from face, fingers with residual shimmer catching morning light on the fingertips.

FACIAL MICRO-DYNAMICS: Eyes opening (from Frame 3 pleasure-close), looking at camera with the satisfied-sharing expression of a tutorial-host showing results, slight knowing-smile (the "see? told you" energy). Lips forming "bas, dekhlo" (enough, see for yourself). Cheekbones GLOWING with product catching the now-warmer morning light (dawn has progressed through the tutorial — warm light increasing as the warmth of the product has increased).

FRAMING: Beauty CU showing full face with completed cheekbone-glow. Camera pulling back slightly from Frame 3 macro to show full effect.

### Frame 5 — Result (Full Glow Reveal)

ASPECT RATIO: 9:16 vertical. SUBJECT: AIRA — [full identity lock]. PRODUCT: Bottle placed on balcony railing beside her, catching full now-warm morning light through amber glass creating golden glow-halo around it. At rest, beautiful, the product as object-in-morning-light-sculpture.

MAKEUP STATE FINAL: Cheekbones glowing with golden-champagne highlighter fully integrated into skin. The "bare-glow" with one strategic addition that transforms the entire face. Morning light now warmer — the highlight catching and AMPLIFYING the growing warmth (the product and the dawn working together).

HAND POSITIONS: Both hands wrapped around a warm mug (chai or coffee — morning ritual object), held at collarbone height. The tutorial is OVER — she is just existing in the morning with her glow. No more teaching, just being.

FACIAL MICRO-DYNAMICS: Eyes — direct soft gaze to camera, no longer teaching but just present, the after-glow-calm of a completed ritual. Slight soft smile. The tender-register at rest. Cheekbones catching morning light and HOLDING it (the product's promise visible in the natural-morning-context). Completely at peace.

FRAMING: MCU portrait with product visible on railing (connection maintained), morning light warm on face, city-below-in-morning-clearing as context.

## VIDEO PROMPTS

# CONCEPT 20 — BEAUTY AD

**Concept Line:** "The shape of want before it becomes a word."
**Format:** Beauty Ad — Beauty Editorial Film
**Product:** Lip oil — sculpted twist non-cylindrical bottle in rose-tinted glass, ergonomic curve in body, brand-mark engraved at base in gold, doe-foot applicator visible when open, interior liquid: sheer berry-rose with light-catching particles, slim elegant silhouette unlike any standard lip product
**Mood Archetype:** MA-9 "the moment before a drop falls"
**Sub-type:** Beauty Editorial Film
**Duration:** 30 seconds total
**Frames:** 6 frames x 5 seconds each
**Register:** KNOWING
**Voice:** SILENT with single whispered fragment "...ruk" at frame 3 (the moment of application)
**Product Move:** P-10 Liquid Materialization (single rose-colored drop appears floating first, then more liquid gathers toward it, coalescing and forming the bottle shape from liquid-state)
**Camera:** Parallax lateral slide revealing depth + slow push-in for application macro
**Setting:** B-2 Wet-Light Bathroom (marble counter, large round backlit mirror, water droplets on glass surface, steam rising from unseen source, reflected wet-surface light play on ceiling, slight humidity haze)
**Wardrobe:** White towel wrapped at chest, bare shoulders and collarbones, damp-skin post-shower aesthetic
**Hair:** HC-22 Towel-Just-Removed — slightly damp, naturally falling, intimate undone
**Makeup:** ML-1 Bare-Glow starting state — the lip oil application IS the beauty moment, arriving at berry-rose glossy lip by final frame
**Color Grade:** Cool bathroom tiles with warm skin priority, slight steam-diffusion, reflected caustic light from water, controlled highlights on wet surfaces, Bradford Young ambient soft reference

## IMAGE PROMPTS

### Frame 1 — Liquid Materialization (Product Birth)

ASPECT RATIO: 9:16 vertical. SUBJECT: AIRA — Adult woman late 20s-early 30s, South Asian (Indian), warm honey-to-caramel skin tone with golden undertone, 5'6"-5'8", soft-strong hourglass-athletic silhouette, fuller sculpted legs with toned thigh definition, fuller shapely thighs, fuller feminine arms with subtle muscle tone, fuller defined chest in proportion, flat toned midsection, defined waist clear waist-to-hip ratio, curvy hip line with natural feminine flare, heart-shaped to oval face, defined cheekbones, full defined lips with natural cupid's bow, almond-shaped expressive eyes dark brown iris with subtle amber flecks, strong but feminine groomed naturally arched brow, natural sun-kissed glow, long dark brown to near-black hair with subtle warm highlights naturally textured soft waves with body and movement, elegant well-groomed hands.

PRODUCT MOVE (P-10): The Liquid Materialization in progress — a single rose-colored drop appears floating at the center of the marble counter surface (5cm above it, hovering), and additional liquid is gathering TOWARD it from multiple directions. Thin streams of berry-rose liquid materialize from the air and converge on the central drop, BUILDING the bottle shape from liquid-state. Currently at 30% formation — the bottom-third of the bottle's sculpted shape is forming as liquid coalesces and solidifies, rose-tinted glass appearing where liquid-mass becomes dense enough to crystallize into solid. The upper portion is still liquid-in-motion, still gathering. The impossible product-birth captured mid-process.

WARDROBE STATE: White towel wrapped at chest (post-shower), tucked at front. Bare shoulders and collarbones exposed, still damp from shower (visible moisture-sheen on skin above towel-line). Intimate, vulnerable, unguarded.

HAIR STATE: HC-22 Towel-Just-Removed — slightly damp, naturally falling in pieces. Not perfectly arranged — some stuck to shoulder/neck (damp-adhesion), some hanging in front, the intimacy of just-out-of-shower hair. Slightly darker at roots from water, lighter at dried-ends.

MAKEUP STATE: ML-1 Bare-Glow — post-shower bare. Skin dewy from steam-and-shower (natural luminosity from hydrated clean skin), lips naturally pink-flushed from hot water (slightly plumped), no product at all. The pre-application state.

HAND POSITIONS: Both hands at counter-edge, resting lightly (she has just arrived at the counter and is watching the materialization happen in front of her). Right hand slightly raised from counter (surprised, fascinated — about to reach forward). Left hand flat on wet marble (grounding in the impossible moment).

FACIAL MICRO-DYNAMICS: Eyes — watching the materialization with fascinated focus (something impossible is happening in front of her), slightly widened, locked on the converging-liquid-forming-bottle at counter-height, the expression between wonder and desire. Brows — slightly raised in fascination. Lips — parted on a held breath (the post-shower-pink natural lips that will receive the product later), the expression of watching something beautiful form. Cheeks — post-shower flush visible on natural skin, steam-dewiness catching bathroom-light. Jaw — slightly dropped from the parted-lip fascination. Breath — held (watching magic).

BODY POSTURE: Standing at marble counter in bathroom, slight forward-lean toward the materializing-product (drawn to it), weight on hands at counter-edge, bare shoulders and collarbones exposed above towel, damp hair falling forward on one side.

KINETIC STILLNESS — Six Layers:
1. Subject micro-action: Eyes locked on materializing-product, right hand lifting from counter 3cm (about to reach), breath held creating total upper-body freeze, the fascination-stillness
2. Fabric/hair state: White towel heavy with slight moisture-weight, static wrapped, damp hair with pieces stuck to skin (neck, right shoulder) not moving (damp-weight holds them), one strand hanging forward from temple
3. Particulate layer: Steam rising from unseen source (recently-used shower visible in background glass), 20+ steam-particles in warm bathroom light creating visible humidity-haze, water droplets on mirror surface behind her catching light as individual bright points, the rose-colored liquid-streams converging-on-central-drop as kinetic-product-particles
4. Contact-point activity: Left palm on wet marble surface (moisture-contact, condensation-wet), counter-edge pressing into both hands, towel-tuck pressing against chest, bare feet on warm bathroom floor (post-shower-warm tile)
5. Background motion: Steam RISING continuously from lower-left (recent shower), water droplets on round backlit mirror catching light and one slowly descending (gravity-drip), slight steam-condensation dripping on glass shower-door in background, the rose-liquid-streams actively converging mid-air toward the forming bottle (the primary kinetic element)
6. Light in motion: Large round BACKLIT mirror creating broad soft rear-illumination (the key-ambient source), steam catching and diffusing this backlight creating visible light-in-steam effect, wet marble surface creating reflected-light-patterns on bathroom ceiling (caustic-water-reflection-play), the rose-colored liquid-streams catching bathroom light and creating tiny moving rose-colored caustics on nearby surfaces as they converge

SPATIAL LOGIC:
- FOREGROUND: Marble counter with wet surface, the materializing-product at center (berry-rose liquid converging and forming bottle-shape — the hero visual). Counter items: minimal (one white ceramic soap dish, folded hand towel). Lower 40% dominated by product-materialization.
- MIDGROUND: Aira at counter, watching, fascinated. Sharp focus (subject and product both in focal plane due to proximity).
- BACKGROUND: Wet-light bathroom — large round backlit mirror (soft warm glow), steam rising, water droplets on glass surfaces, shower-door with condensation, white tile with wet-surface-reflected-light-patterns on ceiling. Soft humid atmosphere.

LIGHTING:
- Key: Large round backlit mirror from behind Aira, creating broad soft back/rim-light (4000K warm-neutral), wrapping around her shoulders and illuminating the steam-haze behind her
- Fill: General bathroom ambient from reflective wet surfaces (marble, tile, glass) bouncing light omnidirectionally at -1 stop from key
- Rim: Mirror-backlight creating strong warm rim on shoulders, hair, and outline separating from steam-background
- Practical: Backlit mirror as visible motivated source, water-surface-reflections creating caustic light-play on ceiling
- Light separation: Subject face 1 stop brighter than surroundings due to wet-skin-reflection catching all available light

FRAMING: MCU with product-materialization as shared hero — lower frame showing marble counter with rose-liquid-converging-to-form-bottle, upper frame showing Aira's fascinated face. Camera at counter-height (product-level). The materialization IS the visual centerpiece.

LENS: 85mm. APERTURE: f/2.0 — product-materialization and Aira's face both sharp (same-distance-plane), steamy background soft with warm diffused bokeh.

COMPOSITION REFERENCE: Bradford Young ambient-soft (Arrival interior-wonder-scenes), beauty-science-fiction-elegance, the impossible-moment framed with reverent naturalism.

ATMOSPHERE: Post-shower steam-intimate-bathroom, warm wet light, the impossible magic of product-formation as contained-wonder-moment, intimate and personal space where something extraordinary happens, beauty as alchemy. Minimal grain (clean polished aesthetic with diffusion from steam).

COLOR GRADE: Cool bathroom tiles as base-temperature, WARM skin-priority (post-shower flush and damp-skin-sheen reading warm against cool environment), rose-pink from materializing-product-liquid as color-accent entering the frame, controlled highlights on all wet surfaces (not blown — contained-gleam), slight overall steam-diffusion creating soft-focus-quality in atmosphere. Bradford Young ambient reference.

NEGATIVE: mirrored, flipped, inverted, extra limbs, fused fingers, melted features, asymmetric eyes (unintentional), garbled text, floating shadows, duplicated subjects, low-res patches, plastic skin, oversharpened, AI-generated artifacts, watermarks, signature, deformed hands, malformed teeth, joint cuts at ankle/knee/wrist/elbow/neck, amputated fingertips, cross-eyed, lazy eye, off-axis pupils, melted clothing, shoes-not-touching-ground, mismatched footwear pair, mannequin-stiff posture, dead eyes, statue-frozen energy, product-materialization looking chaotic (must be elegant convergent), steam below waist, towel falling, product-physics jarring.

### Frame 5 — Video (Mirror Admiration)

SHOT TYPE: MCU over-shoulder into round backlit mirror (seeing her reflection with completed berry-rose lips). CAMERA MOVEMENT: Static with micro-drift (the intimate post-application-mirror-check). LENS: 85mm. SUBJECT ACTION: At 0.0-2.0s she looks at herself in round mirror — the knowing-check (does it look as good as it feels). At 2.0s the slow smile arriving (it does). At 2.5-3.5s slight head-tilt left then right in mirror (checking from angles, seeing how light catches the gloss differently). At 3.5-5.0s direct confident mirror-gaze with full knowing-smile. Product bottle visible held loosely in one hand near collarbone. LIGHTING: Backlit-mirror creating soft glow around her reflection, berry-rose lips catching mirror-light as brightest-feature-in-reflection. AUDIO: Ambient: bathroom settling (steam reducing, drips slowing), slight pleased exhale-through-nose at 2.0s (the satisfaction sound), mirror-light-hum barely audible, steam-condense-drip on glass. Duration: 5 seconds. Frame rate: 24fps.

NEGATIVE: [standard video negative], mirror-angle inconsistent, knowing-smile not arriving naturally, product not visible.

### Frame 6 — Video (Editorial Final)

SHOT TYPE: Beauty MCU portrait. CAMERA MOVEMENT: Final slow push-in (approaching her for the last time, 2cm over 5 seconds, arriving at CU on the knowing-face-with-berry-rose-lips as final image). LENS: 85mm. SUBJECT ACTION: At 0.0-2.0s she places product bottle down on wet marble counter (visible set-down with gentle placement). At 2.0-3.0s one finger touches own lower lip edge (the self-check texture-appreciation-gesture). At 3.0s direct camera-address (not mirror — camera. Breaking the private-moment for one final direct-look at the audience). At 3.5-5.0s the knowing-gaze held with berry-rose lips slightly parted, the single-finger at lip creating intimate framing, steam in background soft, the editorial-final-image held. At 4.5s extremely slight eyebrow raise (the wordless "...told you" expression). Product visible on counter in foreground. LIGHTING: Full bathroom ambient with backlit-mirror as primary, face warmly lit against cool-tile-background, berry-rose lips as the warmest-most-saturated-point in the entire frame, steam diffusing background into soft-focus. AUDIO: Ambient: bathroom acoustics, bottle-set-down on marble (gentle ceramic-on-stone) at 0.5s, absolute settling into silence by 3.0s (the editorial-hold demands complete audio-calm), possible single sustained low-frequency tone barely audible (cinema-texture), held silence through final 2 seconds (the image speaks without sound support). Duration: 5 seconds. Frame rate: 24fps.

NEGATIVE: morphing, warping, identity drift, limb teleport, object pop-in, frame skip, text overlay, watermark, AI artifact, ghosting, double exposure, lip-sync drift, audio desync, wardrobe drift between shots, unmotivated camera shake, physics violation, mannequin posture, frozen background, identity flicker, product not visible in final frame, berry-rose color inconsistent, editorial-mood breaking.
